***эстрадный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эстрадный.html>эстра́дный</a> (14507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эстрада.html>эстра́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">estráda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эстрадный.html>эстра́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">estrádnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> variety, vaudeville

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этажерка.html>этаже́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">etažérka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этажерка.html>этаже́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этажерка.html>этаже́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этажерка.html>этаже́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bookcase, bookshelf <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">furniture displaying books</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>whatnot, a piece of furniture with open shelves for displaying ornaments.</li></ol>

***этак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:этак.html>э́так</a> (6783)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">э-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этак.html>э́так</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">étak</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> so, in this manner, thus
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:этак.html>э́так</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i tak i <b>étak</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this way and that</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> some, about
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:километр.html>киломе́тров</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:этак.html>э́так</a></b> 20</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kilométrov <b>étak</b> 20</i> ― <span class="e-translation">about/some 20 kilometres</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этак.html>э́так</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">étak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> such, like this
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:этакий.html>э́такой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неудача.html>неуда́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pósle <b>étakoj</b> neudáči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">after such a failure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what (a)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:этакий.html>э́такий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́к</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>étakij</b> durák!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what a fool!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***эталон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эталон.html>этало́н</a> (20348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">étalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stalo</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эталон.html>этало́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">etalón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эталон.html>этало́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эталон.html>этало́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эталон.html>этало́нов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">этало́нный</b>)

***это.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> (13)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">étot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">éto</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">nominative neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">étot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: this, it, that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вится</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>éto</b> nrávitsja!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I like it! <i>or</i> I like that!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:свежий.html>све́жее</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:тухлый.html>ту́хлое</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Éto</b> jajcó — svéžeje, a vot <b>éto</b> — túxloje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>This</b> egg is fresh, and <b>this one</b> is rotten.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Éto</b> — učítelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>This</b> is the teacher.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>брат</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Éto</b> — brat i sestrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>They</b> are brother and sister.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кефир.html>кефи́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Éto</b> ne molokó, a kefír</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>This</b> is not milk, but kefir.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">accusative neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">étot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: this, it, that</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>One of the uses of this form is to connect subject and predicate as kind of topic or subject marker. (However, as opposed to actual topic markers such as <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">は</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">wa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in Japanese, ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>’ may be omitted without changing the meaning or breaking the sentence structure.) It does not get translated into English.</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соевый.html>со́евое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a> — (<b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b>) <a href = vnd.unilang:напиток.html>напи́ток</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:полученный.html>полу́ченный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зерно.html>зёрен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соя.html>со́и</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sójevoje molokó — (<b>éto</b>) napítok, polúčennyj iz zjóren sói</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Soy milk is a beverage produced from soybeans.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl>
<ul><li>Note that all of the above examples are ellipses in which the actual verb (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> — is, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>суть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> — are) has been omitted, which is typical for Russian. Oftentimes, the omitted verb is replaced by an em dash.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">éto</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>uh, er, erm, umm; used in hesitant speech
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja, <b>éto</b>, ne kupíl ničevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I, er, I haven't bought anything.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>Части́ца</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>этот</a> (30)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тотъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the expressive prefix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">э-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + | , winning over <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sej</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nineteenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">proximal demonstrative adjective and pronoun</span>, this</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">étude</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этюд.html>этю́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">etjúd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этюд.html>этю́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этюд.html>этю́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этюд.html>этю́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>study, sketch (artwork made in order to practise or demonstrate)</li>
<li>study, etude, exercise</li>
<li>problem</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эфемерный.html>эфеме́рный</a> (30526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">éphémère</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐφήμερος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ephḗmeros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">during one day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эфемерный.html>эфеме́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">efemérnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)эфеме́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)эфеме́рней</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфир</a> (5263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">αἰθήρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aithḗr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upper air</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфи́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">efír</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфи́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфи́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфи́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ether (organic chemistry: a compound containing an oxygen atom bonded to two hydrocarbon groups)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ether</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">alchemy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ether</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">broadcasting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> air
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфи́ре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>efíre</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:эфир.html>эфи́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prjamój <b>efír</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">live broadcast</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">direct ether</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эффективность.html>эффекти́вность</a> (6689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эффективный.html>эффекти́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">effektívnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эффективность.html>эффекти́вность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">effektívnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эффективность.html>эффекти́вности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эффективность.html>эффекти́вности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эффективность.html>эффекти́вностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>effectiveness, efficiency (extent to which time is well used)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:эффективность.html>эффекти́вность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:контроль.html>контро́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>effektívnostʹ</b> kontrólja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">efficiency of controlling</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>efficacy, efficacity</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эшелон.html>эшело́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ešelón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эшелон.html>эшело́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эшелон.html>эшело́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эшелон.html>эшело́нов</a></b>)

<ol><li>echelon</li>
<li>special train, troop train</li></ol>
